***болтать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:болтать.html>болта́ть</a> (3042)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bьltati</i>. Cognate with Polish bełtać ("to stir")
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болтать.html>болта́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">boltátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to dangle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подоконник.html>подоко́ннике</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиде́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:болтать.html>болта́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:джинсы.html>джи́нсах</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершенно.html>соверше́нно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:незнакомый.html>незнако́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дядька.html>дя́дька</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na podokónnike sidél i <b>boltál</b> nogámi v džínsax soveršénno neznakómyj djádʹka.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">On the window sill sat an a complete stranger, in jeans, <b>dangling</b> his feet.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to shake, to rock, to stir</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stir, to mix, to beat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:литый.html>ли́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мгновение.html>мгнове́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перестать.html>переста́ла</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:болтать.html>болта́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ложка.html>ло́жкой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:похлебка.html>похлёбку</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Líta na mgnovénije dáže perestála <b>boltátʹ</b> lóžkoj poxljóbku.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Lita in an instant even stopped <b>beating</b> her soup with a spoon.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to babble, to talk needlessly or endlessly</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to converse</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:болтаться.html>болта́ться</a> (4558)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болтать.html>болта́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boltátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***болтливый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:болтливый.html>болтли́вый</a> (17086)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болтать.html>болта́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boltátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ли́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болтливый.html>болтли́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">boltlívyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)болтли́вее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)болтли́вей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> talkative</li>
<li>blabbing <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">prone not to keep secrets</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>боль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bolь</i>.

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>боль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ница</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больница.html>больни́ца</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bolʹníca</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больница.html>больни́цы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больница.html>больни́цы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больница.html>больни́ц</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:больно.html>больно</a> (1497)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolʹnój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больно.html>бо́льно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bólʹno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bad, badly</li>
<li>painfully</li>
<li>extremely, terribly</li>
<li>a bit too</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>боль</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bolʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bolʹnój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Predicative">Predicative</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больно.html>бо́льно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bólʹno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> it is painful, it hurts
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:больно.html>бо́льно</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne <b>bólʹno</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">it hurts me, I am in pain</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>боль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ной</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-noj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bolʹnój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)больне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)больне́й</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sick, ill</li>
<li>painful</li>
<li>weak</li>
<li>morbid</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:большинство.html>большинство́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolʹšinstvó</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">majority</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-вик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***большевистский.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:большевистский.html>большеви́стский</a> (10013)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From an ephemeral <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">большеви́ст</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolʹševíst</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> which has however reached persistent prominency in other languages as <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bolschewist</i>. While the form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:большевистский.html>большеви́стский</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolʹševístskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> has, with help by the Soviet ruling class, attained exclusivity, the exiled enemies of the reds – including in Germany – have continued to use the form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">большеви́цкий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolʹševíckij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, regularly derived from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:большевик.html>большеви́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolʹševík</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:большевистский.html>большеви́стский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bolʹševístskij</span>)
</p>

***большой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́й</a> (62)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bel-</i>, whence Ancient Greek <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">βελτῐ́ων</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">beltíōn</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">better</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bolʹšój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)бо́льше</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:больший.html>бо́льший</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наибольший.html>наибо́льший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>big, large, great
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зал.html>зал</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bolʹšój</b> zal</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>large</b> hall</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>больша́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:буква.html>бу́ква</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bolʹšája</b> búkva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">capital letter</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>big</b> letter</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>больша́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bolʹšája</b> doróga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">highroad, highway, main road</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>great</b> road</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчик</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bolʹšój</b> málʹčik</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>big</b> boy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>больша́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:москва.html>москва́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bolʹšája</b> Moskvá</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Greater</b> Moscow</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́й</a></b> ло́ндон</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bolʹšój</b> Lóndon</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Greater</b> London</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́лец</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руки́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bolʹšój</b> pálec právoj rukí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">right thumb</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>big</b> finger of the right hand</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́лец</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:левый.html>ле́вой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>ноги́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bolʹšój</b> pálec lévoj nogí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">left <b>big</b> toe</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:театр.html>теа́тр</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Bolʹšój</b> teátr</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bolshoi_Theatre" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bolshoi Theatre">Bolshoi Theatre</a></span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>great</b> theater</span>”)</div></dd>

***бомж.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бомж.html>бомж</a> (9359)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Acronym of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a> <b>б</b>ез <b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></b>пределённого <b>м</b>е́ста <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>ж</a></b>и́тельства</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">licó <b>b</b>ez <b>o</b>predeljónnovo <b>m</b>ésta <b>ž</b>ítelʹstva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> - a person without defined place of residence.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бомж.html>бомж</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bomž</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бомж.html>бомжа́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бомж.html>бомжи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бомж.html>бомже́й</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">бомжи́ха</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tramp, bum, hobo, slacker, homeless person</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> poorly dressed person
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>Из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приличный.html>прили́чной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:семья.html>семьи́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>хо́дит</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бомж.html>бомжо́м</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Iz prilíčnoj semʹí, a xódit <b>bomžóm</b>!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He’s from a decent family, but dresses like a bum!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***бон.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бон.html>бон</a> (14112)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">bon</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бон.html>бон</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bon</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бон.html>бо́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бон.html>бо́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бон.html>бо́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>voucher</li>
<li>bon (an early type of paper currency)</li>
<li>any paper currency collected by notaphilists</li></ol>

***бондарь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бондарь.html>бондарь</a> (24540)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бондарь.html>бо́ндарь</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бондарь.html>бонда́рь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bóndarʹ</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bondárʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бондарь.html>бо́ндаря</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бондарь.html>бондаря́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бондарь.html>бо́ндари</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бондарь.html>бондари́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бондарь.html>бо́ндарей</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бондарь.html>бондаре́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cooper <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">craftsman who manufactures large bowls, barrels or ship masts</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***бордюр.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бордюр.html>бордю́р</a> (29714)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">bordure</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бордюр.html>бордю́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bordjúr</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бордюр.html>бордю́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бордюр.html>бордю́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бордюр.html>бордю́ров</a></b>)
</p>
